Patrick Mahomes real test as an elite QB will be when he doesn't have multiple elite offensive players to throw to. 50% of his "magic" throws would turn into more interceptions more frequently without players like Hill to chase after them down the field. Mahome's is good but in reality he hasn't even been tested yet. All this "future all time great" hype talk needs to stop until he's actually tested for a few seasons without an elite offense. People are going to feel really stupid if he fizzles out once his top receivers are gone. He has the equivalent of what Brady has in Tampa Bay except Mahomes was lucky enough to get that in his first few years in the league. Brady went 6 years without a Superbowl run. Mahomes hasn't even been tested with that kind of mental stress yet season after season. I can't say anything other than he's a great QB because saying anything else other than that sounds ridiculous.
